country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.10
	title = ww1_italy.10.t
	desc = ww1_italy.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		date > 1911.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ITA_you_can_stop_now
		}
		tag = ITA
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.10.a
		activate_mission = ITA_countdown_until_no_libya
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_countdown_until_no_libya_tt
		activate_mission = ITA_nationalist_media_pressure
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_support < 0.6
			}
			add_war_support = 0.03
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_political_power_var = -0.01
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_war_pp_loss = 0.01
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_war_pp_display = 1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_we_want_a_war
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.002
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.002
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.12
	title = ww1_italy.12.t
	desc = ww1_italy.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_luigi_luzzatti
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	# Accept Ultimatum
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.12.a
		ITA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.38
				days = 1
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR
					OR = {
						state = 448
						state = 450
						state = 1060
						state = 1061
						state = 661
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = ITA
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = TUR
					OR = {
						state = 663
						state = 273
						state = 1122
						state = 1124
						state = 1128
						state = 1128
						state = 567
						state = 754
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = LBA
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				TUR = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = ITA
						ratio < 0.6
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Reject Ultimatum
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.12.b
		ITA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.37
				days = 1
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = blank
		effect_tooltip = {
			ITA = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = TUR
					type = take_claimed_state
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#Offer Italy protectorates
		name = ww1_italy.12.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = historical_tt
		ITA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.25
				days = 1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = effects_if_accept_ITA
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = TUR
					OR = {
						state = 448
						state = 1060
						state = 661
						state = 273
						state = 567
						state = 1061
						state = 450
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = TRP
			}
			TRP = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = TUR
					relation = military_access
					active = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = empty_focus
			}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_government = communism
		}
		date > 1912.7.3
		tag = ITA
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.32.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						ITA_maximalist_power = ITA_reformist_socialist_power
					}
					check_variable = {
						ITA_maximalist_power > ITA_reformist_socialist_power
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = ww1_italy.52
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					ITA_maximalist_power < ITA_reformist_socialist_power
				}
			}
			country_event = ww1_italy.53
		}
	}
}

#post giolitti
country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.61
	title = ww1_italy.61.t
	desc = ww1_italy.61.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ita_giolitti_elected
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.61.a
		clr_country_flag = ITA_vote_of_no_confidence_flag
		complete_national_focus = ITA_fall_of_the_great
		#Salandra Conservative Tree
		# ITA_salandra
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = ITA_ally_the_catholic_electoral_union
				check_variable = {
					ITA_left_wing_focuses_taken < -1
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_sal_suces
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.69
				days = 2
			}
		}
		#Radical Tree
		# ITA_radicals_in_power
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = ITA_leftist_union
				has_completed_focus = ITA_bring_radicals_into_government
				check_variable = {
					ITA_right_wing_focuses_taken < -1
				}
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = ITA_church_as_tool_of_the_state
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.298
				days = 2
			}
		}
		#Luigi luzzatti wahoo
		# ITA_the_compromise_that_pleases_none
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = ITA_ally_the_catholic_electoral_union
					has_completed_focus = ITA_leftist_union
				}
				has_completed_focus = ITA_male_suffrage
				has_completed_focus = ITA_sway_economic_experts
				has_completed_focus = ITA_shore_up_the_classic_liberals
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.297
				days = 2
			}
		}
		# Pollio
		# ITA_like_father_like_son
		#else_if = {
		#	limit = {
		#		NOT = {
		#			has_completed_focus = ITA_full_male_suffrage
		#			has_completed_focus = ITA_ally_the_catholic_electoral_union					#liberal union
		#			has_completed_focus = ITA_leftist_union					#leftist union
		#			has_global_flag = pollio_dies
		#		}
		#	}
		#	country_event = {
		#		id = ww1_italy.318
		#		days = 2
		#	}
		#}
		# Sonnino
		# ITA_consensus_of_the_divided
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = ITA_ally_the_catholic_electoral_union					#liberal union
					has_completed_focus = ITA_leftist_union					#leftist union
					has_completed_focus = ITA_sway_economic_experts
					has_completed_focus = ITA_shore_up_the_classic_liberals
				}
				has_completed_focus = ITA_full_male_suffrage
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.336
				days = 2
			}
		}
		# Murri
		# ITA_christian_democracy2
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = ITA_leftist_union
				has_completed_focus = ITA_church_as_tool_of_the_state
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.340
				days = 2
			}
		}
		# Leonida 
		# ITA_democratic_socialism
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = ITA_leftist_union
				check_variable = {
					ITA_right_wing_focuses_taken = 0
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.345
				days = 2
			}
		}
		# Enrico Corradini
		# ITA_a_dark_horse_emerges
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = ITA_ally_the_catholic_electoral_union
				check_variable = {
					ITA_left_wing_focuses_taken = 0
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.355
				days = 2
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = pollio_dies
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_italy.318
					days = 2
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_sal_suces
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					long_name = ITA_democratic_party
					name = ITA_democratic_party
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = ITA_antonio_salandra
					ideology = liberal_conservatism
				}
				complete_national_focus = ITA_ascension_of_the_destra
				complete_national_focus = ITA_salandra
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.96
	title = ww1_italy.96.t
	desc = ww1_italy.96.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = ITA_treaty_of_ouchy
		clr_global_flag = ITA_not_done_libya_war
		set_global_flag = libyan_crisis_resolved
		set_global_flag = italo_turkish_war_ends
		hidden_effect = {
			white_peace = TUR
			white_peace = LBA
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_ally_with = TUR
						AND = {
							tag = LBA
							has_war_with = ITA
						}
					}
				}
				white_peace = ITA
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ally_with = ITA
				}
				white_peace = TUR
			}
			# TUR = {
			# 	diplomatic_relation = {
			# 		country = LBA
			# 		relation = guarantee
			# 		active = no
			# 	}
			# }
			LBA = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = TUR
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				set_country_flag = italo_turkish_war_winner
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_libya.6
					days = 5
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = TUR
					has_state_flag = fallen_to_italy_ITA_TUR_war
				}
				transfer_state_to = ITA
				add_claim_by = ITA
				if = {
					limit = { 
						is_core_of = TUR 
					}
					remove_core_of = TUR
					add_claim_by = TUR				
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_state = {
						is_owned_by = TUR
						has_state_flag = fallen_to_italy_ITA_TUR_war
					}
				}
				activate_mission = ITA_return_rhodes_mission
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = TUR
					OR = {
						state = 448
						state = 450
						state = 1060
						state = 1157
						state = 1156
						state = 663
						state = 1061
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = ITA
				add_claim_by = ITA
				if = {
					limit = { 
						is_core_of = TUR 
					}
					remove_core_of = TUR
					add_claim_by = TUR				
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_resistance = yes
						has_global_flag = libyan_compliance
					}
					add_compliance = 20
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = TUR
					is_core_of = LBA
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						is_core_of = TUR 
					}
					remove_core_of = TUR
					add_claim_by = TUR				
				}
				transfer_state_to = LBA
			}
			LBA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ITA
					modifier = hostile_status
				}
			}			
			TUR = {
			    if = {
				    limit = {
					    has_country_flag = TUR_italo_turkish_war_arab_minorities
				    }
			        every_state = {
				        limit = {
					        is_core_of = LBA
					        has_state_flag = TUR_removed_libyan_minority
				        }
				        set_state_flag = TUR_arab_state
			        }
			    }
			    #delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Trablusgarp Milisi" }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = LBA
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
				country_event = { id = ww1_ottoman.138 days = 90 }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					region = 225
				}
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = { original_tag = TUR }
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
			}
			ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.96.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			LBA = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ITA
					modifier = large_decrease
				}
			}
			white_peace = TUR
			white_peace = LBA
			ITA = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_libya.6
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
		news_event = ww1_italianturkish.10
	}
}

		}

				}

		}
	}

									is_owned_by = LBA
									is_claimed_by = ROOT
								}
							}
						}			
					}

				}

							is_owned_or_subject_PREV_trigger = yes
						}
					}
					has_global_flag = ITA_london_ubari
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = ITA_london_tunisa
						has_global_flag = ITA_france_will_help_you
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = ITA_london_tyrol_and_istria
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = ITA_london_expand_istria

					has_global_flag = ITA_london_tyrol_and_istria
				}

					has_global_flag = ITA_london_dalmatia

					NOT = {

			base = 500
		}
	}

		}

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = ITA_london_tyrol_and_istria

		}

			}

						}

		}

		if = {

			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_london_eat_tunisa
		}
		else = {

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = blank
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_unlock_treaty_london
		set_global_flag = ITA_london_unlock
		clr_global_flag = ongoing_negotiations_ITA

				has_global_flag = ITA_london_dalmatia_2_yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_global_flag = ITA_london_tunisa_yes
			}
			modifier = {

				has_global_flag = ITA_london_ubari_yes
			}

				has_global_flag = ITA_london_naval_agreement_yes
			}

			}
			modifier = {

#Entente - Equipment
country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.200
	title = ww1_italy.200.t
	desc = ww1_italy.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = ITA_london_stockpiles
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.200.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_british_pov_thing
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_london_stockpiles
		
		set_global_flag = ITA_london_stockpiles_yes
		effect_tooltip = {
			send_equipment = {				
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = 10000
				target = ITA
			}
			send_equipment = {				
				type = field_gun_equipment
				amount = 800
				target = ITA
			}
			send_equipment = {
				type = howitzer_equipment
				amount = 200
				target = ITA
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.201
				days = 1
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_equipment = {
				infantry_equipment > 10000
			}
			has_equipment = {
				field_gun_equipment > 800
			}
			has_equipment = {
				howitzer_equipment > 200
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 35
				FROM = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment < 2500
					}
					has_equipment = {
						field_gun_equipment < 250
					}
				}
				has_equipment = {
					infantry_equipment > 20000
				}
				has_equipment = {
					field_gun_equipment > 2000
				}
				has_equipment = {
					howitzer_equipment > 500
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.200.b
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.202
				days = 1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				has_equipment = {
					infantry_equipment < 10000
				}
				has_equipment = {
					field_gun_equipment < 1000
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				FROM = {
					has_equipment = {
						infantry_equipment > 10000
					}
					has_equipment = {
						field_gun_equipment > 1000
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.281
	title = ww1_italy.281.t
	desc = ww1_italy.281.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_army_ww1
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		is_great_war_ongoing = yes
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_war_with = AUS
				war_length_with = {
					tag = AUS
					months > 5
				}
				NOT = {
					controls_province = 9598
					controls_province = 6675
					controls_province = 6626
					controls_province = 3674
					controls_province = 12888
				}
			}
			AND = {
				has_war_with = FRA
				war_length_with = {
					tag = FRA
					months > 5
				}
				NOT = {
					controls_province = 9603
					controls_province = 3768
					controls_province = 9909
					controls_province = 11969
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.281.a
		IF = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = ITA_call_a_party_conference
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_war_score_minus_7
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = 0.007
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				ITA_percieved_usefulness = -7
			}
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = ITA_a_red_future
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.288
	title = ww1_italy.288.t
	desc = ww1_italy.288.d
	picture = GFX_bleriot_ix_plane
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.288.a
		add_political_power = 10
		air_experience = 5
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					has_tech = fighter1
				}
			}
			create_production_license = {
				target = ITA
				equipment = {
					type = fighter_equipment_1
				}
				cost_factor = 0
			}
		}
		ITA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.289
				days = 2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				#so dem/neutral france accepts dem/neutral italy
				FRA = {
					OR = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
				ITA = {
					OR = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				has_same_ideology = yes
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				FRA = {
					OR = {
						has_government = communism
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				ITA = {
					has_same_ideology = yes
				}
				add = 1000
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.288.b
		add_political_power = -5
		ITA = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_italy.290
				days = 2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FRA = {
					OR = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
				ITA = {
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							has_government = democratic
							has_government = neutrality
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				FRA = {
					OR = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				ITA = {
					has_same_ideology = no
				}
				add = 1000
			}
		}
	}
}

#france accepts
country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.289
	title = ww1_italy.289.t
	desc = ww1_italy.289.d
	picture = GFX_bleriot_ix_plane
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.289.a
		set_country_flag = ITA_french_accepted_license_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Arms Against Tyranny"
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_mio_tt
			show_mio_tooltip = ITA_macchi_organization
			mio:ITA_macchi_organization = {
				add_mio_size = 2
			}
		}
		else = {
			air_experience = 15
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_designer
			show_ideas_tooltip = societa_anonima_nieuport_macchi
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space_tt
		unlock_decision_tooltip = ITA_build_nieuport_fighters
		custom_effect_tooltip = when_taken
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_build_nieuport_fighters.tt
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_war_with = ENT
			has_war_with = GER
		}
		OR = {
			is_in_faction_with = GER
			is_in_faction_with = ENT
		}
		original_tag = ITA
		OR = {
			communism > 0.45
			surrender_progress > 0.6
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = ITA_demobilize_the_army
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.395.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_above_50_warning
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.395.b

			limit = {
				has_war_with = ENT
			}
			ENT = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_italy.396
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = GER
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_italy.396
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_war_peace_effec
	}
}

					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {

				}
			}

		}

				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					original_tag = ROOT
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				give_military_access = PREV
			}

			level = 5
		}

					id = ww1_italy.397
					days = 2
				}

					start = 0
					end = 4

						limit = {
							industrial_complex > 0
						}
						remove_building = {
							type = industrial_complex
							level = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_italy.455
	title = ww1_italy.455.t
	desc = ww1_italy.455.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_italian_soldiers_in_libya
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.455.a
		add_ideas = ITA_treaty_with_italians
		FROM = {
			country_event = ww1_italy.456			
			if = {
				limit =  {
					tag = HBY
				}
				set_country_flag = protectorate
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomous_state = autonomy_tgwr_informal_protectorate
				}		
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					tag = MJT
				}
				set_country_flag = protectorate
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomous_state = autonomy_tgwr_informal_protectorate
				}					
			}
			else = {
				puppet = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ww1_italy.456
	title = ww1_italy.456.t
	desc = ww1_italy.456.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy.456.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_ideas = ITA_treaty_with_italians
			}
			puppet = FROM
			if = {
				limit =  {
					FROM = {
						tag = HBY
					}
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = FROM
					autonomous_state = autonomy_tgwr_protectorate
				}
				set_country_flag = protectorate
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					FROM = {
						tag = MJT
					}
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = FROM
					autonomous_state = autonomy_tgwr_informal_protectorate
				}
				set_country_flag = protectorate
			}
		}
	}

	id = ww1_italy_war.1
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		casualties_k > 10
		OR = {
			has_war_with = AUS
			has_war_with = FRA
		}
	}
	option = {
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_percieved_usefulness = -1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_useful_minus_1
	}
}

	#title = ww1_italy_war.179.t
	#desc = ww1_italy_war.179.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		OR = {
			GER = {
				casualties_inflicted_by = {
					opponent = ITA
					thousands > 790
				}
			}
			ENG = {
				casualties_inflicted_by = {
					opponent = ITA
					thousands > 790
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				casualties_inflicted_by = {
					opponent = ITA
					thousands > 790
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				casualties_inflicted_by = {
					opponent = ITA
					thousands > 790
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				casualties_inflicted_by = {
					opponent = ITA
					thousands > 790
				}
			}
			TUR = {
				casualties_inflicted_by = {
					opponent = ITA
					thousands > 790
				}
			}
			BUL = {
				casualties_inflicted_by = {
					opponent = ITA
					thousands > 790
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = AUS
			has_war_with = FRA
		}
	}
	option = {
		#name = ww1_italy_war.179.a
		add_to_variable = {
			ITA_percieved_usefulness = 1
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = HBY
					original_tag = MJT
					original_tag = GLD
				}
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = ITA_treaty_with_italians
				remove_ideas = ITA_treaty_with_italians2
				remove_ideas = ITA_exiled_sultan
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ITA
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			ROOT = {
				end_puppet = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GLD = {
					exists = no
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				release_on_controlled = GLD
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ITA
				OR = {
					state = 559
					state = 880
				}
			}
			THIS = {
				transfer_state_to = GLD
			}
		}
	}
}

			has_country_flag = great_war_loser

		}
		has_war = no
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 15
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_iw_italy.61.a
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			long_name = ITA_democratic_liberal_union_party
			name = ITA_democratic_liberal_union_party
		}
		promote_character = ITA_giovanni_giolitti
	}
}

			remove_advisor_role = {
				slot = political_advisor
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader={
					ideology=fascism_ideology
					traits = {
						il_duce
					}	
				}
				promote_leader = yes
			}
			set_portraits = {
				civilian = {
					large="gfx/leaders/ITA/ITA_benito_mussolini.png"
				}
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = fascism
			long_name = ITA_fascism_fasces_party_long
			name = ITA_fascism_fasces_party
		}
		set_global_flag = fascism_created
	}
}

country_event = {
	# Reset navy variables 1910
	id = ww1_italy_dev.1
	title = ww1_italy_dev.1.t
	desc = blank
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_italy_dev.1.a
		set_variable = {
			ITA_industrial_capacity_dockyard = -0.25
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_speed = -0.5
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_naval_defense_factor = -0.45
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_org = -0.45
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_see_subs = -0.15
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_oopsies = 0.25
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_exp = -0.45
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_weather = 0.4
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_metal_shark_bite = -0.1
		}
		set_variable = {
			ITA_navy_visible_on_surface = 0.05
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		}

		}
	}

		}
	}
	option = {

		add_to_variable = {

		}
	}
